content="1785"/></p></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-12" itemprop="description" v-pre><p><b>Angels' Share</b> by <b>By Kilian</b> is a Oriental Vanilla fragrance for women and men. <b>Angels' Share</b> was launched in 2020. The nose behind this fragrance is Benoist Lapouza. Top note is Cognac; middle notes are Cinnamon, Tonka Bean, Oak and Hedione; base notes are Vanilla, Praline, Sandalwood and Candied Almond. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>"Introducing a new olfactive family, Kilian Hennessy pays tribute to his heritage, as heir to the renowned French cognac-making family, and to his choice olfactory intoxicants for driving the night towards dawn.</p>

<p>A first-time collaboration with French perfumer Benoit Lapouza, the perfume Angel's Share is Kilian Hennessy's most personal fragrance creation yet, inspired by his eighth-generation inheritance of Hennessy savoir-faire in cognac making. The perfume goes deep into the cellars of founder's mind and memory, and into its most mysterious dimension: "la part des anges" or "angels' share"— an evaporation of liquor in oak barrels that lifts, while aging, like a silent offering to the gods.<br />
<br />
Much like a Master Perfumer who crafts accords and essences in a perfume, a Master Blender combines the eaux-de-vie in perfect proportions for an exceptional cognac. Angels' Share contains the essence of Cognac derived from the liquor to lend it a natural caramel color. Opening with cognac oil, upon a blend of oak absolute, cinnamon essence and Tonka bean absolute, the scent's long-lasting notes of sandalwood, praline and vanilla make for a delicious finish, a rare concoction only angels should experience."<br />
<br />
<strong>Notes: </strong>Cognac, Tonka Bean and Oak wood.<br />

A hint of tonka is added.<br />
<br />
It's the only one in the Ambre Narguilé / Oajan / Angels' Share trio in which I truly and very strongly smell apple and for once, I therefore agree; yes, it smells like apple pie (I don't know if there really is apple but the effect is striking!).<br />
<br />
A very caramelized apple pie, heavily sprinkled with cinnamon that leans towards Tarte Tatin (but not exactly because remember that there is neither cinnamon nor cognac in the latter).<br />
<br />
I like it, it's nice, it smells good but we are here in a pure gourmandise, so be careful if you can't tolerate this kind of perfume; Angels' Share is a pastry, a real one!<br />
<br />
For my part, my favorite of the three remains Oajan which is - according to my personal tastes - 'tuned' to perfection. But now that I've been able to smell them all, I have to say that I find them quite different.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2321475"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2321475#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2321386" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1219108">GloryRide</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-15">10/15/24 02:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My first <b>By Kilian</b> sample. <br />
<br />
This smells good and delectable, it's well blended and hard to dislike. You have to really like potent frags and sweet things in order for this to win you over though. I'm sure I detected a hint of <i>liquorice</i> in this? Be as it may, the individual notes aren't so easily detectable at first, or then this makes me a bit noseblind.<br />
<br />
After the opening <b>AS</b> changes into a more forward fragrance where it really makes its sweet presence known, maybe in a bit too forward manner for my liking. It isn't juvenile by any means but still quite "screaming", I wouldn't wear this indoors with semi-formal fashion but rather only outside with a jacket during the cold months. It's potent to the point of being disturbing.<br />
<br />
Owning a pre-reformu-batch of <b>Oajan</b> by <b>PDM</b>, imo <b>AS</b> is somewhat similar to it but still does it's own thing. Both are good but I prefer (older batch) Oajan for its more refined nature, as well as that Oajan isn't as potent and synthetic.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This is it! <br />
<br />
After months of waiting, I finally ordered a 100ml bottle of this magic. <br />
<br />
It is straight up, apple pie with custard and candied brandy balls. <br />
<br />
It’s rich, luxurious, smooth, potent and sweet! <br />
<br />
The spice to me isn’t so much a ‘woody’ spice - more so a sweeter cinnamon kind of vibe, which makes it perfect for this time of year. <br />
<br />
Personally, I find this so addictive that I just can’t but help overspray it whenever I wear it. The performance is amazing. Throughout the day you will wafts of this as you’re encapsulated inside a sweet scent bubble. <br />
<br />
It is gourmand and it is sweet, but not synthetic or juvenile. It’s quite sophisticated and develops on the skin nicely.  For me, the sweet notes are enhanced on the dry down and I can’t stop smelling myself. <br />
<br />
This fills a room easily and is a compliment magnet, as it leaves a beautiful and distinctive sillage. I couldn’t wear this everyday as it is very sweet and I would sicken myself with it, but whenever I do wear it - I just can’t get enough!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Superb job Killian, this is your best creation and also one of the best creations on the market.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2308568"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2308568#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306956" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1836514">Oxana123456789</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 05:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It took me time to appreciate this perfume. But once I did, it is love! <br />
<br />
The scent is indescribable. Some smell apple pie, some smell sweet woodiness. To me it is explosion of freshly chopped wood with distant apple vanilla coziness and with a slight boozy character. But this is not an intoxicating alcohol that one drank, it is more like a story of very well made cognac. <br />
<br />
The name comes from the belief: when cognac seeps through the oak barrels, this what called angel's share. This part of the cognac goes to angels. I love this story. <br />
<br />
I do not drink alcohol anymore. I am happy to accept the Angel’s Share! This is wonderful. <br />
<br />
The perfume has impressive longevity. It lasts on the clothes forever. Another great quality (for me) - it does not have patchouli! All perfumes with patchouli smell the same on my clothes after a few days. And that smell is a granny smell. Old woman in theatre who pulled out of the closet with moth balls some old garment and sprayed strong domineering punchy elixir to be festive. I do enjoy many perfumes that contain patchouli note, but I do not like their after-smell. All individuality is lost and “the granny” comes out. <br />
<br />
Angel’s Share does NOT dry out as “the granny”. It’s more of a vanilla/sandalwood dry out. Very soft and calm. <br />
<br />
It is a masterpiece and honestly I do not know any rival!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2305548"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2305548#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305155" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you like almond you will like LOVE this since it's definitely the centre point of this fragrance.<br />
<br />
I can certainly smell the praline and oak in hear as well, pairs very well with everything.<br />
<br />
The sweetness of the cinnamon-y vanilla balances the perfume out perfectly.<br />
<br />
An interesting fragrance, not personally my cup of tea, but it's pleasant to smell, and if a close friend had this as their signature scent I would enjoy the smell of it everytime we hugged.<br />
<br />
Not super strong, longevity isn't bad, not intense but also not subtle.<br />
<br />
Something to wear on a night out, or christmas market evenings. This is cognac and cinnamon done to perfection. This DNA is almost guaranteed to yield great results, and in this case with an added intoxicating twist. On initial spray to me is a sweet and sharp booze which quickly dries down to its famous 'apple pie' scent profile. The projection is there, mainly because of how it can cut through the cold, and its longevity is not bad either: about 6 hours on my skin. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2280816" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Shimmer412"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1889185"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1889185.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Shimmer412" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Kayali-Fragrances/The-Wedding-Silk-Santal-36-83208.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.83208.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Wedding Silk Santal | 36"title="The Wedding Silk Santal | 36"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2280816ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2280816" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1889185">Shimmer412</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-12">09/12/24 15:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very Beautiful, Sweet, warm, boozy, deep, spicy, woody, and super cozy and comforting.<br />
<br />
Oh WOW, ok so this is really very beautiful! I honestly didn’t expect to love this as much as I do… I’m definitely impressed! To me it smells like a warm cinnamon apple pie with boozy and woody notes. I’m not sure what’s giving me an apple scent, but I’m getting one. The cognac brings a golden boozy warmth throughout. The cinnamon is also prominent throughout with its sweet and warm spicy scent. The tonka bean and vanilla bring more warmth as well as a soft touch of creaminess. The oak and sandalwood add a lovely and comforting woody scent. I do pick up a little bit of the candied almond scent, but it’s subtle.<br />
<br />
Definitely a fragrance I consider best suited for fall and winter. There’s a really lovely warm, cozy, and comforting feel to this that just screams fall and winter to me… when all is chilly and colorful outside, but warm and comfortable inside. I picture being wrapped in a cozy sweater or blanket next to a warm fire (no, I don’t get a smoky scent) with my favorite book, a cup of spiked hot apple cider, an apple pie baking in the oven, and looking out the window at the chilly rain coming down on all of the colorful leaves and pine cones in the trees.<br />
<br />
I get exceptional performance with Angels’ Share. The longevity is fantastic, it lasts the entire day and I can still smell it the next morning. The projection is great too, it radiates out at least a few feet from me. I only need a few sprays to get this effect, so I do consider this to be a good value.<br />
<br />
It reminds me just a little bit of Skylar Fall Cashmere and Kayali Lovefest Burning Cherry. I don’t have many fragrances that are like these ones, but this is one that I think many people would enjoy having as part of their collections!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; So in defense of shamelessly ripped off anrtists everywhere, here it is again: JEAN-CLAUDE ELLENA.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2275783"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2275783#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275716" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2275716" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fragrantlyenhanced"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453129"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1453129.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="fragrantlyenhanced" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2275716ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2275716" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453129">fragrantlyenhanced</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-08">09/08/24 06:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'll start off by saying I dislike gourmands. But this stood out to me a lot because of the boozy, smoky quality. Of course, the cinnamon apple pie comparison has been made. It really does smell like that. Super accurate. Reminds me a lot of the crust that is baked to perfection. Like, if it would've been in the oven for just a minute longer, it would've burnt. It still leans a bit too sweet for my tastes, but it's bearable. Super warm and nutty, creamy with a slight burnt caramel touch. It is quite strong, so please, be easy on the trigger. It doesn't need your help with over-spraying lol<br />
<br />
I can understand why people really love this fragrance because it is really cozy, musky, and can hit some strong memory associations of grandma's apple pie. I won't lie, I was repressing an involuntary chewing motion with my jaw HAHA. And I guess that's what great perfumery is all about, really. Something beyond just smelling nice. It's an emotional experience. You smell something that just evokes a feeling or hits you with a core memory that replays the whole experience in the back of your head. Great combination of notes. I enjoyed it, but I really, really cannot wear gourmands. But please, wear this for me if you're into it. I love smelling it in the air.<br />
<br />
Made me chew air/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2275716"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2275716#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275316" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2273942" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="glorianne99"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1725067"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1725067.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="glorianne99" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2273942ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2273942" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1725067">glorianne99</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-06">09/06/24 14:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My review comes from the experience of wearing this about 5 times using (1) a sample from LuckyScent and (2) the perfume tester from Sephora. <br />
<br />
The opening of this perfume is strongly reminiscent of the cognac and cinnamon notes. The cinnamon is so strong in the opening that it's almost a peppery smell which is not my favorite. However, it quickly dries down to something just incredibly special. Sweet, warm, and cozy apple pie. More accurately, in fact, the warm fried cinnamon apple slices from Cracker Barrel. This smells EXACT to these fried apple slices in astonishing accuracy. This makes sense as there are no notes in this perfume that would relate to the pie crust in apple pie. This is next on my buy list, I must have it especially for the holidays. This fragrance perfectly emanates the sweet, shy girl who lives at the library and spends her time with her nose in a book and drinking tea, and maybe some knitting. By no means am I saying this scent is “granny-ish”, although I could see any age completely rocking this scent from 18-80. The sweetness in the dry down makes this fragrance enticing for younger crowds as well.<br />
<br />
I somehow have actually become emotionally attached to this perfume. This is the fragrance you wear when you are kind of sad and need some comfort. Or are cold and feeling cozy in fall or winter. Or feeling sentimental. The comment by avion saying they cried when they first smelled it makes sense to me now. There is something so reminiscent of childhood nostalgia about this wonderful fragrance that creates a somehow positively associated “homesick” experience. Others enjoy smelling this on you as well. <br />
<br />
Longevity:at least 5 hours<br />
Sillage: profound, per the remarks of others who were at least 10 feet away.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2273942"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2273942#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2270593" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1339079">avion</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 16:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have never written a review before. But after 350ml of this, I couldn’t resist.<br />
<br />
I have been using Angels’ Share for a while now. I cried the first time I smelled it. <br />
<br />
It smells nostalgic. It smells like that perfect day from your childhood. <br />
<br />
It is winter break and life is good. School is over and it is snowing outside. You wake up in the morning to the smell of your grandma’s warm cinnamon buns. Straight out of oven. You can’t resist and take a bite, although your mom is telling you that you should finish breakfast first.<br />
<br />
Everything is perfect. The gifts are under the tree. Your granddad sitting on his wooden rocking chair smoking a pipe. Your little sister watching old Disney Christmas animated films (Chip and Dale to be accurate). Your father preparing your sled as your mother is helping you wear your winter clothes. Life is good.<br />
<br />
You go out at the usual time to play with your friends. You play till the warm lights come on. From building a snowman to sledging down a hill. Nostalgia has a way of incorporating weeks of activities in a single memory of a single day. <br />
<br />
You come back to a warm home as the ice melts off your gloves. Your dad and grandpa are having a cognac by the fireplace while they talk about topics you couldn’t care less about, nevertheless, you’re still happy to be there. Your grandma is knitting and your sister is asleep on the couch.<br />
<br />
Your mother helps you put on your pyjamas — the ones with letters and numbers and you sit by your dad and eat the last cinnamon left. Later you get carried to bed as you fell asleep watching Mickey’s Christmas Carol. Life will never be as good as it is right in this moment. You just don’t know it yet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2267464"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2267464#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2266991" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The one thing that still shocks me is that Angels Share even outperforms my bottle of PDM Haltane which lasts all day on my skin. Even though my brother and I try to make fun of each other's collections, I admit the smell is heavenly and it is a projection beast. The scent opens up with a boozy and woody accord and reminds me of the opening to Replica Jazz Club. It then beautifully dries down to become a more warm, vanilla spice scent. I love this fragrance and the bottle, but my only two problems are the price and the lack of versatility. Even my brother admits it isn't a fragrance you can wear to work, school and most gatherings. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2258284" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="na.conrad"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1409224"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1409224.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="na.conrad" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giardini-Di-Toscana/Bianco-Latte-64757.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.64757.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bianco Latte"title="Bianco Latte"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2258284ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2258284" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1409224">na.conrad</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-23">08/23/24 07:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Angels’ Share is a fragrance that immediately draws you in with its rich, intoxicating scent. The moment you spray it, the cognac note comes through strong, setting the stage for what feels like a luxurious experience. It’s warm, inviting, and instantly makes you think of something aged and refined.<br />
<br />
The heart of this fragrance unfurls with the spice of cinnamon, followed by the deep tones of tonka bean and oak. It’s cozy and comforting, reminiscent of apple pie moonshine or warm spiked cider—a scent that warms you from the inside out. The boozy cognac paired with the sweetness of vanilla gives it a mature, sophisticated edge that’s both elegant and delicious.<br />
<br />
The dry down is where Angels’ Share truly shines. The vanilla and praline add a soft sweetness, while the sandalwood keeps it grounded. The scent is perfect for those cooler months when you want something that feels warm and luxurious, like wrapping yourself in a soft blanket on a chilly evening.<br />
<br />
Kilian has truly captured the essence of “la part des anges” with this fragrance. It’s a scent that feels indulgent and special, like a rare treat you savor slowly. If you’re looking for something that’s rich, cozy, and a little bit boozy, Angels’ Share is definitely worth trying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2258284"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2258284#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2256935" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2217799">bee888</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-12">08/12/24 19:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Upon first application, the cognac (of course) was a bit strong and disarming, but as my wear time increased, the tonka bean and vanilla came out to play. <br />
<br />
The cinnamon is questionable - you can definitely smell it, and it works well with the other notes by adding a hint of spice and interest into an otherwise very sweet perfume, but gets lost after a couple of hours of wear. Which, actually, I don't mind - it was one of my less favored parts of the perfume, but I respect its presence somehow.<br />
<br />
When I saw that other reviewers mentioned there might be a toothpaste smell after a couple of hours, somehow I get it. It might be the sandalwood? It's like if you smelled a smear of toothpaste that's been dried for a day or so - not actually minty, but more of a smell of the other ingredients in it.<br />
<br />
Overall, a decent gourmand scent. The longevity is quite strong, lasting 8+ hours for me with just small dabs. Most likely would not purchase for myself, but glad I tried.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2247287"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2247287#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2246813" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/720808">matereac9</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-10">08/10/24 05:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I opened the packaging and got a whiff of the "in the bottle" smell I immediately thought I wouldn't like it. In the bottle it smells like a mixture of spiced, cold apple juice, and generic "perfume smell". I wasn't going to try it, but I'm very glad I did!<br />
I sprayed it, then I gave it half an hour and went back for a sniff, and I cried. It smelt just like my Grandma and Grandads house at Christmas. Apple pie, cinnamon, cognac, chocolates, and a tiny hint of smoke in the background. Something in this comes through as marzipan for me which I adore. It's very sweet, but not sickly so, it's balanced and just scrummy. It has a playful, childhood scent that is calmed and matured by the boozy brandy and cinnamon. The sandalwood takes it just into unisex sweetness, rather than feminine. <br />
<br />
I adore this. I've got plenty of perfumes that invoke good memories and plenty that I consider firm favourites, but this is something else. Never have I had a scent bring me to tears, it is SO emotional for me. I'm hoping that this one just gets better as it ages! <br />
<br />
I didn't think I was really a signature scent kind of person, although I've always desperately wanted to find something that people will remember me wearing when I'm long gone. It turns out I just hadn't found my signature yet ❤️<br />
<br />
Oh, and I can't possibly write this without special mention of my cat, who absolutely ADORES this fragrance, and constantly rubs against my wrists and my neck when I use this, and if she gets on my perfume shelf she'll rub the bottle! 🤣</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; At first smell, I wasn't very fond of it, and I had to test it at least like 4 or 5 times to get used to it and appreciate it for what it really is. Angels share might be the best gourmand scent I've encountered, better than vanilla diorama for me. The notes all complement each other in this which I like, it's an incredible mix of woody notes, some cognac, and that beautiful cinnamon and tonka bean combination, which dries down into a sweet praline with vanilla. It can definitely come off very feminine if you're trying it for the first time, but after smelling it more and more, I think its very unisex, and anyone can pull this off. Might be the best winter scent you can have. If only it wasn't so expensive.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2237248"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2237248#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2237032" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Well now it’s the middle of summer, and my best good friend recently became obsessed with Angels Share &amp; talks about her love for it so much that I decided to give it another try, and I am pleasantly surprised.<br />
<br />
It almost smells like apple pie but it doesn’t. It’s sweet, friendly &amp; playful. It makes me happy to smell like this. It last several hours on skin, which is rare for perfumes these days. <br />
<br />
I can’t decide which season this is best for. I didn’t like it in the winter but I like it now in the summer time. Seems mixed up. So I’m going to say it might be good year round, just not during holiday parties where apple pie will be served.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2234485" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="eylulcnar"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1681408"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1681408.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="eylulcnar" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2234485ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2234485" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1681408">eylulcnar</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-31">07/31/24 04:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This perfume holds memory at each person, you have just not lived that scene yet. A friend of mine and I was visiting Graz in Austria, in which there was a HUGE perfume store. As we were walking around, this particular perfume and its bottle caught my eye. You guessed it, it was Angel's share. I've read about it online and heard all the hype, so I was eager to get my hands on it. Me and my friend took a sniff and looked at each other with wide-open eyes. This is PURE cinnamon roll-bottled in. I didn't get alcohol notes AT ALL, which is a plus for me. The woody cinnamon with the vanilla was a perfect signature for a cold winter day, as it was snowing outside and this fragrance made our chest warm. <br />
<br />
Definitely the FIRST unisex perfume that is ACTUALLY unisex. It reminds me of a wealthy husband and wife who owns a pub that is also a casino, the room is lit with candles. They both wears this perfume. The woman wears a fur jacket and has put on red lipstick, whereas the man wears gold rings and has a laughter that aged like a wine. <br />
<br />
It delivers a story, a message and a memory all in one spray. <br />
<br />
10/10 in my book. Will definitely buy it once I have the financial capability. if you have the budget, get this. if you can authenticate and get this at a cheaper price, get it. when people say angels share is above its dupes, it really is. <br />
<br />
the first time i smelled this in store, i couldnt stop thinking about it. its a very boozy cozy apple pie with cinnamon. in the dry down, you get the vanilla.<br />
<br />
i own khamrah and i would say that khamrah does a good job. if you dont wanna spend so much on angels share then get khamrah (or sharaf blend?). the main difference i would say is that khamrah is much heavier and you get a very middle eastern twist to it due to the dates and nutmeg probably. angels share is way wayyy boozier and i would say much lighter.<br />
<br />
despite the huge price difference, i cant say that one is better than the other. i prefer angels share as its lighter for me, but khamrah is still a very nice scent. ill continue to use khamrah as my room freshener as its cheaper HAHAH.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2229183" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="curlycomedy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2014858"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2014858.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="curlycomedy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lattafa-Perfumes/Lail-Maleki-59133.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.59133.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lail Maleki"title="Lail Maleki"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2229183ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2229183" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2014858">curlycomedy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-25">07/25/24 12:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not trying to be contrarian, but I do not get apple pie or any hint of apple. I don’t even get a gourmand here. I get pepper and then smoke—like it is a flanker of By the Fireplace by Maison Margiela - and that black pepper brings to mind KFC mashed potatoes (not an insult), which makes it feel as cozy as comfort food. I get woods and something a little plastic like adhesive bandages. Finally as it dries down I get a prominent powder scent mixed in with the peppery opening. I am not dunking on this fragrance at all. I am sure as my nose evolves I will pick out some of the notes listed. I don’t get sweet, but I don’t get so savory that I am in a cab where someone just finished eating takeout. More earthy, woodsy, mature, unisex-to-masculine. I like it before bed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2229183"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2229183#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2228451" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Sweet baked apple along with woodiness. It is not a loud perfume, it hovers softly around me but longevity is impressive. Usually when I spray perfume on my skin, it disappears pretty fast while holding on clothes longer. Angels Share stayed on my skin for many hours and on my clothes for at least 24 hours and counting. I do not get nose blind to it which is a rarity. It is comforting, inviting. I would not call it sickly sweet, although it is sweet. I got travel size and I am thinking about full bottle. But before I jump, I want to see if I get tired of it.<br />
Update: I got quite obsessed with it during two days of wearing. However I did not quite like it all the time. My absolutely favorite is Miss Dior EDP 2021 and I decided to compare them side by side. I was very surprised to smell Miss Dior next to Angels Share. Angels Share was sweet warm apple, while Miss Dior was very complex in comparison. I gave my husband to smell both papers (blindly) asking which why he liked more. He first smelled Angel Share and had this puzzled look. I asked him does he smell anything. He said: “Oh, I do! It smells like… something chemical” I gave him Miss Dior tester and he said: “Oh, this is much more sophisticated! <br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Projection: 7/10<br />
Smell: 10/10<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/605809">Emma0714</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-12-01">12/01/20 03:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Angel's Share is the most luxurious gourmand I own. Opens up with warm apples, covered with caramelized brown sugar, and lots and lots of cinnamon. Warm apple pie, straight from the oven. When the pie cools down, you can smell warm woods - almost that sauna smell, mixed with the scents of a christmas fair - wafts of candied apples and caramelized nuts. And open fires? It smells a little bit toasy or burnt, and I mean that in the good way. I don't get dried fruit/grapes/raisin for the cognac at all, only apples. And it's not nearly as boozy as the packaging suggests, but if any I'd say its more calvados than cognac. <br />
<br />
Lovely fragrance, perfect for the autumn and holiday season! If you are into warm and cuddly fragrances, you need to try this. People will defenitly wanna hug you for a few seconds longer with this one on!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1255113"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1255113#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1262967" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1262967" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jarrid_steel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1242708"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1242708.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jarrid_steel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rabanne/1-Million-Prive-37698.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.37698.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="1 Million Privé"title="1 Million Privé"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1262967ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1262967" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1242708">jarrid_steel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-12-19">12/19/20 07:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I LOVE this fragrance. A few weeks ago I was fortunate enough to get a sample of both Angel's Share and Roses on Ice. When I returned home, I sprayed my right hand with Angel's Share and my left with Roses on Ice. Roses on Ice is beautiful but I feel as though it leans more feminine but Angel's Share just blew me away. I could not stop smelling my right hand. <br />
<br />
After about 30 minutes, my mind was made up. I e-mailed the By Kilian specialist at my local Holt Renfrew to put aside a bottle for me as I would only be able to return to the store the next weekend. He replied back and with pleasure, said he would save me a bottle. But it was the last one in stock at any of the Holt Renfrews. He was getting e-mails and calls from other Holt's around Canada, asking him for the bottle he had in stock and he refused, as he had already promised his last bottle to me. <br />
<br />
Seeing how this is sold out everywhere you look, I'm very thankful and appreciative to him for hiding away the bottle for me. When I went to the store last Saturday to pick up the bottle, he had literally hidden it in the bottom of one of the cupboards of his booth, at the bottom of a shopping bag in which he was storing tester cards, so that no one would find it and sell it when he wasn't at work. He went above and beyond to make sure that bottle was mine and I am thrilled and feel extremely blessed to own it. It is my first By Kilian and to date, the most expensive fragrance in my collection. <br />
<br />
Now, on to the performance. <br />
<br />
On my skin, this stuff is a beast. It radiates a good 5-6 feet away. It leaves an intoxicating scent trail as I walk and it lasts FOREVER. It was my scent of the day yesterday (Friday) and this morning as I am typing this, I am STILL catching wafts of it, although much fainter, over 24 hours after spraying it. In fact, it is actually 27 hours since I first sprayed it on. So, even though it is by far the most expensive perfume in my collection, ($300 CAD for 50ml), a little goes a LONG way, which makes this a much better value than some other perfumes that were much less expensive but last a fraction of the time. <br />
<br />
I am in love with this fragrance. Boozy, woody, sweet, sexy. It is just absolutely perfect for this time of year. I don't think you could pull this off in the warmer months because the sweetness might get cloying but during the colder parts of fall, spring and definitely throughout the winter, this fragrance will cut through the cold and make a huge impression on everyone around you. <br />
<br />
In my opinion, this is an absolute masterpiece. 10/10 fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1262967"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1262967#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1526752" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2267464" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="avion"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1339079"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1339079.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="avion" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Tobacco-Vanille-1825.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1825.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Tobacco Vanille"title="Tobacco Vanille"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2267464ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2267464" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1339079">avion</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 16:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have never written a review before. But after 350ml of this, I couldn’t resist.<br />
<br />
I have been using Angels’ Share for a while now. I cried the first time I smelled it. <br />
<br />
It smells nostalgic. It smells like that perfect day from your childhood. <br />
<br />
It is winter break and life is good. School is over and it is snowing outside. You wake up in the morning to the smell of your grandma’s warm cinnamon buns. Straight out of oven. You can’t resist and take a bite, although your mom is telling you that you should finish breakfast first.<br />
<br />
Everything is perfect. The gifts are under the tree. Your granddad sitting on his wooden rocking chair smoking a pipe. Your little sister watching old Disney Christmas animated films (Chip and Dale to be accurate). Your father preparing your sled as your mother is helping you wear your winter clothes. Life is good.<br />
<br />
You go out at the usual time to play with your friends. You play till the warm lights come on. From building a snowman to sledging down a hill. Nostalgia has a way of incorporating weeks of activities in a single memory of a single day. <br />
<br />
You come back to a warm home as the ice melts off your gloves. Your dad and grandpa are having a cognac by the fireplace while they talk about topics you couldn’t care less about, nevertheless, you’re still happy to be there. Your grandma is knitting and your sister is asleep on the couch.<br />
<br />
Your mother helps you put on your pyjamas — the ones with letters and numbers and you sit by your dad and eat the last cinnamon left. Later you get carried to bed as you fell asleep watching Mickey’s Christmas Carol. Life will never be as good as it is right in this moment. You just don’t know it yet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="2267464"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=2267464#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="62615" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1095199">Bubbles1964</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-01-03">01/03/21 16:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If you are like me, and you thought you missed something special this past year, fear not. <br />
<br />
I bought a 3ml decant of Angels’ Share after I saw it show up on lists and in the Fragrantica year end awards. I’ve had the opportunity to wear it a few times and I’m left underwhelmed. <br />
<br />
One of the worst descriptors I can write in a fragrance review is generic, and that’s what Angels’ Share is to me: a sugary, boozy, tonka-infused vanilla nothing burger. Certainly not great, definitely not niche, and absolutely the reason why I’m pushing the  “ok” button.<br />
<br />
Edit: wore it again and into the dislike bin it goes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1270058"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1270058#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1676706" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1676706" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Dzarsos"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/632677"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.632677.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Dzarsos" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/The-Merchant-of-Venice/Colonia-Veneziana-60399.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.60399.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Colonia Veneziana"title="Colonia Veneziana"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1676706ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1676706" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/632677">Dzarsos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-10-29">10/29/22 07:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Picture this:<br />
You wake up in a well-off stranger's bed, after over-indulging at an upscale soiree of some sort. Bleary-eyed and reeling slightly, stale liquor on your breath, you get dressed, and, without saying a word to your bedmate, you stumble to the door and "sneak" out into the blinding sun. <br />
<br />
Staggering towards your home, you're about midway through your "definitely too old for this sh*t" walk-of-shame, with your suit jacket still emanating whiffs of whatever VSOP or XO you spilt on it the night before, when you spot a bakery. Your stomach gives an insistent lurch, and, rather than finishing your journey home, to take a couple of ibuprofen and drink some water like an adult, you decide to tackle your hangover with a slice of pie - apple, for preference. <br />
<br />
Now sat in a corner booth, ignoring or oblivious to the parents shooting you dirty looks, as your head keeps bobbing slightly with your hung-over dizziness, you jump a bit as a plate is placed in front of you. Half-smiling, you take a deep whiff of the pie you ordered - à la mode, to your delight - and for a moment, apple, cinnamon, and vanilla overpower the cognac you reek of. <br />
<br />
Missing your own mouth slightly, you manage to take a bite, slowly masticating your questionable breakfast, and starting to feel vaguely human. But as you swallow, the booze scent rises again, this time accompanied by the smear of vanilla ice cream your drunk ass has left under your nose - in response, your headache throbs, your stomach gurgles, and as a baby starts to cry in the far corner, you feel the stirrings of genuine regret.<br />
<br />
This is what Angels' Share smells like to me.<br />
<br />
Indeed, while I personally haven't lived through that sort of situation in a number of years, the booze-and-vanilla of the opening, combined with the mild headache I already had when I sprayed this on, made me feel exactly like I used to in similar such mornings, around the tail end of my party days.<br />
<br />
Now, I suppose, if you are in the habit of smelling like drink anyway, Angels' Share has strong potential for being a high-end cover-up - but, to my nose, this is not something I would ever wear. I would - maybe - spray it in a room the morning after a get-together, to freshen things up a little, but is a pretty strong "maybe" - it might just exacerbate everyone's hangover.<br />
<br />
And, of course, this is not an air freshener - it's a very expensive (and kind of surprisingly well-regarded) perfume. In that capacity, however, it fails my nose completely, as it just makes me smell like a *kind of* high-class drunk - and then continues to do so for hours on end, as this stuff has annoyingly incredible longevity. <br />
<br />
So, in the end, it's a strong "no" from me - I can't deny the quality, so it does get a small boost from that, but ultimately, I am a grown man, and I have no desire to smell like a "morning after" party boy anymore - not even a super classy one. <br />
5.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1676706"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1676706#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1894364" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1549907">restein</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-07">12/07/22 11:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>wow, I can't believe this gets such high ratings! It smelled like the apartment of an elderly alcoholic with a slowly escalating hoarding problem to me. But then there's this minty scent that makes it smell like that person tried to cover things up by cleaning a bit.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1704153"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1704153#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1275719" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1275719" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="charmedbella"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/157401"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.157401.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="charmedbella" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/Libre-56077.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.56077.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Libre"title="Libre"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1275719ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1275719" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/157401">charmedbella</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-01-14">01/14/21 03:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I bought this blind when it became available on the Kilian website.  Very boozy in the opening.  The dry down is all "mint toothpaste".  I just couldn't unsmell it.  Returned to Kilian because it's too expensive to hang on to.  Too boozy and toothpaste-y for me.  Extremely over-hyped.<br />
<br />
I was really hoping for the apple pie some others have experienced, but alas, I was condemned to an alcoholic toothpaste.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="62615"comment_id="1275719"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/By-Kilian/Angels-Share-62615.html?ccid=1275719#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="62615" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
